It a Disney’s Characters Parade!!! n not just any Disney Parada..its a Disney Fluffy Parada shoffi enti ba2a! >_<

The marching bands’ that lead the parade have these big cartoonish looking musical instrumets which they play one of the best marching musical pieces that gives the feeling of Excitement, expectations and just Charming! The sound of the Parade’s music fills the place as everyone out there gives attention to the Fluffiest Disney Parade ever!!

Poo’s eyes were glowing and sparkling as she was watching the parade approaching them with the marching back in the front and the rest are yet to follow..at this point it was not clear yet who/what was behind after the Band. Poo was very excited what happens next, with all this Lovely Marching Music “LMM” and the Bands beautiful Eye catching customs and their funny looking instruments, who wudnt be excited in such a situation!! The Shella also share this feeling with Poo, Happiness, Fluffiness and Excitement for whats goin to be next!

The band passes on while still continuing to play their Lovely Music and the Characters Start showing Up!!! >_<

Poo’s heart skips a beat from how excited she is!! She first sees a Handsome looking Guy in a lovely Slim suit “mesh a7la men beta3et Flynn” and he is ridding an old Fashioned convertible car holding a mic and announcing that this Parade is very special and Fluffy in its own way and he explained how:
“
The purpose of this Lovely Parade Ladies and Gentle men is not to only let you see our beloved Disney Characters, but to make you live among them and getting to the Disney Dream!! So this Parade will have 10 of the Most Beloved Disney characters among other characters, each one of these 10 will pick RANDOMLY someone from you to get to spend the next hour with them during the Parade!!! 
Thank you Ladies and Gentle men, Enjooy ;)”

People all around can’t believe their ears of what was just said! Spending an hour with a Disney Character and living the Parade experience!! Who wudnt want that!!

Poo mesh messada2a heya Kaman ya 7aram!! And she was just imaging herself living that Beautiful and indeed Fluffy Dream, she just had lil doubt that she might not be lucky enough to get picked by random!
Which what Flynn at this very moment noticed in her eyes since eno byfhamha men 3eneeha ma3 en 3eneeha mesh shabah 3een el se7leya zy nas! :D :p

Poo can’t believe her eye..she can believe that she’s within close viewing distance with...
